# stat.ML [[Back]](#toc)

### [122] [Generalization error bounds for two-layer neural networks with Lipschitz loss function](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06281)
*Jiang Yu Nguwi,Nicolas Privault*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 该论文推导了双层神经网络训练中的泛化误差界，不假设损失函数有界，使用Wasserstein距离估计和随机梯度方法的矩界，在独立测试数据下获得维度无关的O(n^{-1/2})收敛率，非独立情况下获得O(n^{-1/(d_in+d_out)})收敛率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有神经网络泛化误差分析通常假设损失函数有界，这限制了理论的应用范围。作者旨在推导不依赖损失函数有界假设的泛化误差界，为实际训练提供更通用的理论保证。

Method: 使用Wasserstein距离估计概率分布与其经验测度之间的差异，结合随机梯度方法的矩界分析。通过概率分布差异的量化来推导泛化误差界，特别处理独立和非独立测试数据两种情况。

Result: 在独立测试数据情况下获得维度无关的O(n^{-1/2})收敛率，在非独立情况下获得维度相关的O(n^{-1/(d_in+d_out)})收敛率。所有边界及其系数可在模型训练前显式计算，并通过数值模拟验证了理论结果。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了不依赖损失函数有界假设的神经网络泛化误差理论框架，为实际训练提供了可计算的先验误差界，特别是在独立测试数据下获得了维度无关的有利收敛率。

Abstract: We derive generalization error bounds for the training of two-layer neural networks without assuming boundedness of the loss function, using Wasserstein distance estimates on the discrepancy between a probability distribution and its associated empirical measure, together with moment bounds for the associated stochastic gradient method. In the case of independent test data, we obtain a dimension-free rate of order $O(n^{-1/2} )$ on the $n$-sample generalization error, whereas without independence assumption, we derive a bound of order $O(n^{-1 / ( d_{\rm in}+d_{\rm out} )} )$, where $d_{\rm in}$, $d_{\rm out}$ denote input and output dimensions. Our bounds and their coefficients can be explicitly computed prior to the training of the model, and are confirmed by numerical simulations.

</details>


### [123] [Tight Convergence Rates for Online Distributed Linear Estimation with Adversarial Measurements](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06282)
*Nibedita Roy,Vishal Halder,Gugan Thoppe,Alexandre Reiffers-Masson,Mihir Dhanakshirur,Naman,Alexandre Azor*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究分布式参数服务器-工作者设置中的随机向量均值估计问题，主要挑战包括：1) 对抗性测量（部分工作者可能传输损坏的测量值）；2) 异步性（每次只有一个工作者活跃）。这些问题在分布式传感和网络断层扫描等应用中具有重要意义。

Method: 采用两时间尺度的ℓ₁最小化算法，在已知传感矩阵A满足零空间性质类条件下进行分析。先前工作建立了渐近恢复结果，本文则建立了紧致的非渐近收敛速率，并识别了A的松弛条件。

Result: 在相同零空间性质类条件下建立了紧致的非渐近收敛速率。识别了A的松弛条件，在这些条件下精确恢复可能失败，但E[X]的投影分量恢复仍然可能。提供了对抗性工作者分布式线性估计中鲁棒性、可识别性和统计效率的统一有限时间刻画。

Conclusion: 该工作为具有对抗性工作者的分布式线性估计提供了统一的有限时间理论框架，阐明了鲁棒性、可识别性和统计效率之间的关系，对网络断层扫描和相关分布式传感问题具有重要应用价值。

Abstract: We study mean estimation of a random vector $X$ in a distributed parameter-server-worker setup. Worker $i$ observes samples of $a_i^\top X$, where $a_i^\top$ is the $i$th row of a known sensing matrix $A$. The key challenges are adversarial measurements and asynchrony: a fixed subset of workers may transmit corrupted measurements, and workers are activated asynchronously--only one is active at any time. In our previous work, we proposed a two-timescale $\ell_1$-minimization algorithm and established asymptotic recovery under a null-space-property-like condition on $A$. In this work, we establish tight non-asymptotic convergence rates under the same null-space-property-like condition. We also identify relaxed conditions on $A$ under which exact recovery may fail but recovery of a projected component of $\mathbb{E}[X]$ remains possible. Overall, our results provide a unified finite-time characterization of robustness, identifiability, and statistical efficiency in distributed linear estimation with adversarial workers, with implications for network tomography and related distributed sensing problems.

### [124] [A Data-Informed Variational Clustering Framework for Noisy High-Dimensional Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06864)
*Wan Ping Chen*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: DIVI是一个数据驱动的变分聚类框架，针对高维噪声数据，结合全局特征门控和基于分裂的自适应结构增长，实现稳定聚类、特征相关学习和模型复杂度自适应调整。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在高维噪声环境下进行聚类面临多重挑战：只有少量维度具有信息性、聚类数量未知、特征噪声严重。传统的基于似然的方法在这种情况下容易变得不稳定或对噪声维度过于敏感。需要一种能够同时处理分区恢复、特征相关性学习和结构自适应的方法。

Method: DIVI框架结合了全局特征门控和基于分裂的自适应结构增长。它使用信息性先验初始化来稳定优化过程，以可微分方式学习特征相关性，并且仅当局部诊断表明模型欠拟合时才扩展模型复杂度。该方法还考虑了运行时可扩展性和参数敏感性。

Result: 在严重特征噪声下，DIVI表现出有竞争力的聚类性能，计算上可行，产生可解释的特征门控行为，同时展现出保守的增长模式和在挑战性设置中可识别的失败机制。

Conclusion: DIVI最好被视为针对噪声高维数据的实用变分聚类框架，而不是完全贝叶斯生成解决方案。它在处理高维噪声数据时提供了稳定、可解释且计算可行的聚类方法。

Abstract: Clustering in high-dimensional settings with severe feature noise remains challenging, especially when only a small subset of dimensions is informative and the final number of clusters is not specified in advance. In such regimes, partition recovery, feature relevance learning, and structural adaptation are tightly coupled, and standard likelihood-based methods can become unstable or overly sensitive to noisy dimensions. We propose DIVI, a data-informed variational clustering framework that combines global feature gating with split-based adaptive structure growth. DIVI uses informative prior initialization to stabilize optimization, learns feature relevance in a differentiable manner, and expands model complexity only when local diagnostics indicate underfit. Beyond clustering performance, we also examine runtime scalability and parameter sensitivity in order to clarify the computational and practical behavior of the framework. Empirically, we find that DIVI performs competitively under severe feature noise, remains computationally feasible, and yields interpretable feature-gating behavior, while also exhibiting conservative growth and identifiable failure regimes in challenging settings. Overall, DIVI is best viewed as a practical variational clustering framework for noisy high-dimensional data rather than as a fully Bayesian generative solution.

### [125] [Amortized Filtering and Smoothing with Conditional Normalizing Flows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07169)
*Tiangang Cui,Xiaodong Feng,Chenlong Pei,Xiaoliang Wan,Tao Zhou*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: AFSF：基于条件归一化流的统一摊销框架，用于高维非线性动力系统的贝叶斯滤波和平滑


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高维非线性动力系统的贝叶斯滤波和平滑是科学和工程中的基础但具有挑战性的问题，需要开发能够处理复杂动态的有效方法。

Method: 提出AFSF框架，使用循环编码器将观测历史映射到固定维度的摘要统计量，基于此共享表示学习前向流（用于滤波分布）和后向流（用于后向转移核），通过标准后向递归恢复整个轨迹的平滑分布。

Result: AFSF能够准确近似滤波分布和平滑路径，通过学习底层时间演化结构支持超出训练范围的推断，并通过共享摘要统计量在潜在状态轨迹上引入隐式正则化，提高轨迹级平滑性能。

Conclusion: AFSF为高维非线性动力系统的贝叶斯滤波和平滑提供了一个有效的统一摊销框架，结合了条件归一化流的灵活性和循环编码的时间序列处理能力。

Abstract: Bayesian filtering and smoothing for high-dimensional nonlinear dynamical systems are fundamental yet challenging problems in many areas of science and engineering. In this work, we propose AFSF, a unified amortized framework for filtering and smoothing with conditional normalizing flows. The core idea is to encode each observation history into a fixed-dimensional summary statistic and use this shared representation to learn both a forward flow for the filtering distribution and a backward flow for the backward transition kernel. Specifically, a recurrent encoder maps each observation history to a fixed-dimensional summary statistic whose dimension does not depend on the length of the time series. Conditioned on this shared summary statistic, the forward flow approximates the filtering distribution, while the backward flow approximates the backward transition kernel. The smoothing distribution over an entire trajectory is then recovered by combining the terminal filtering distribution with the learned backward flow through the standard backward recursion. By learning the underlying temporal evolution structure, AFSF also supports extrapolation beyond the training horizon. Moreover, by coupling the two flows through shared summary statistics, AFSF induces an implicit regularization across latent state trajectories and improves trajectory-level smoothing. In addition, we develop a flow-based particle filtering variant that provides an alternative filtering procedure and enables ESS-based diagnostics when explicit model factors are available. Numerical experiments demonstrate that AFSF provides accurate approximations of both filtering distributions and smoothing paths.

</details>


### [126] [The Theory and Practice of Highly Scalable Gaussian Process Regression with Nearest Neighbours](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07267)
*Robert Allison,Tomasz Maciazek,Anthony Stephenson*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文为最近邻高斯过程（NNGP/GPnn）回归建立了完整的理论框架，证明了其在大样本下的统计性质，包括点预测收敛性、一致性、达到最优收敛速率以及对超参数调优的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高斯过程回归因其立方计算复杂度难以应用于大规模数据集。虽然最近邻高斯过程（NNGP/GPnn）方法在实践中表现出色，但其大样本理论尚不完整，需要建立严格的理论基础来支持其作为可扩展高斯过程替代方案的合理性。

Method: 建立NNGP/GPnn回归的理论分析框架，在温和的正则性假设下，推导三个关键预测指标（均方误差MSE、校准系数CAL、负对数似然NLL）的几乎必然点收敛极限。研究L2风险，证明普遍一致性，并分析收敛速率。同时证明MSE在紧凑超参数集上的一致收敛性及其对超参数导数的渐近性质。

Result: 证明了NNGP/GPnn回归的几乎必然点收敛性；建立了普遍一致性；风险达到Stone极小极大速率n^{-2α/(2p+d)}；MSE在紧凑超参数集上一致收敛；MSE对长度尺度、核尺度、噪声方差的导数渐近消失，解释了GPnn对超参数调优的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 为NNGP/GPnn回归提供了严格的统计理论基础，证明其作为高度可扩展且原理性强的全高斯过程模型替代方案的合理性，特别强调了其对超参数调优的鲁棒性优势。

Abstract: Gaussian process ($GP$) regression is a widely used non-parametric modeling tool, but its cubic complexity in the training size limits its use on massive data sets. A practical remedy is to predict using only the nearest neighbours of each test point, as in Nearest Neighbour Gaussian Process ($NNGP$) regression for geospatial problems and the related scalable $GPnn$ method for more general machine-learning applications. Despite their strong empirical performance, the large-$n$ theory of $NNGP/GPnn$ remains incomplete. We develop a theoretical framework for $NNGP$ and $GPnn$ regression. Under mild regularity assumptions, we derive almost sure pointwise limits for three key predictive criteria: mean squared error ($MSE$), calibration coefficient ($CAL$), and negative log-likelihood ($NLL$). We then study the $L_2$-risk, prove universal consistency, and show that the risk attains Stone's minimax rate $n^{-2α/(2p+d)}$, where $α$ and $p$ capture regularity of the regression problem. We also prove uniform convergence of $MSE$ over compact hyper-parameter sets and show that its derivatives with respect to lengthscale, kernel scale, and noise variance vanish asymptotically, with explicit rates. This explains the observed robustness of $GPnn$ to hyper-parameter tuning. These results provide a rigorous statistical foundation for $NNGP/GPnn$ as a highly scalable and principled alternative to full $GP$ models.

</details>


### [127] [Gaussian Approximation for Asynchronous Q-learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07323)
*Artemy Rubtsov,Sergey Samsonov,Vladimir Ulyanov,Alexey Naumov*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 论文推导了异步Q学习算法中Polyak-Ruppert平均迭代的高维中心极限定理收敛速率，使用多项式步长k^{-ω}，在均匀几何遍历马尔可夫链假设下，获得超矩形类上高达n^{-1/6}log^4(nSA)的收敛速率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用多项式步长k^{-ω}（ω∈(1/2,1]），假设状态-动作-下一状态三元组序列形成均匀几何遍历马尔可夫链。证明了一个关于鞅差和的高维中心极限定理作为关键技术工具，用于分析Polyak-Ruppert平均迭代的收敛行为。

Result: 在超矩形类上获得了高达n^{-1/6}log^4(nSA)的收敛速率，其中n是算法使用的样本数，S和A分别是状态和动作的数量。此外，还给出了算法最后迭代的高阶矩界限。

Conclusion: 论文建立了异步Q学习算法中Polyak-Ruppert平均迭代的高维中心极限定理收敛速率，证明了在均匀几何遍历马尔可夫链假设下，可以获得多项式收敛速率。提出的高维鞅差和中心极限定理具有独立的理论价值。

Abstract: In this paper, we derive rates of convergence in the high-dimensional central limit theorem for Polyak-Ruppert averaged iterates generated by the asynchronous Q-learning algorithm with a polynomial stepsize $k^{-ω},\, ω\in (1/2, 1]$. Assuming that the sequence of state-action-next-state triples $(s_k, a_k, s_{k+1})_{k \geq 0}$ forms a uniformly geometrically ergodic Markov chain, we establish a rate of order up to $n^{-1/6} \log^{4} (nS A)$ over the class of hyper-rectangles, where $n$ is the number of samples used by the algorithm and $S$ and $A$ denote the numbers of states and actions, respectively. To obtain this result, we prove a high-dimensional central limit theorem for sums of martingale differences, which may be of independent interest. Finally, we present bounds for high-order moments for the algorithm's last iterate.

### [130] [The Chambolle-Pock method also converges weakly with $0 < θ\le 1$ and $τσ\|L\|^{2} < 4θ(2-θ)/(1 - 2θ+ 9θ^{2} - 4θ^{3})$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06423)
*Manu Upadhyaya*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 该论文扩展了Chambolle-Pock方法的收敛理论，证明了在更广泛的松弛参数范围(0<θ≤1/2)下的弱收敛性，并给出了新的步长条件保证O(1/k)的遍历对偶间隙收敛率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Chambolle-Pock方法是凸凹鞍点问题和复合凸优化的标准一阶算法，但现有的收敛理论主要关注θ>1/2的情况。对于0<θ≤1/2这一先前未探索的参数区域，缺乏系统的收敛性分析，需要建立统一的收敛理论框架。

Method: 在实Hilbert空间中研究Chambolle-Pock方法，考虑步长τ,σ>0和松弛参数0<θ≤1。基于Lyapunov函数方法，构建在整个参数区间0<θ≤1上保持一致的收敛性证明框架，分析遍历对偶间隙的收敛率和原始-对偶迭代的弱收敛性。

Result: 证明了当τσ|L|² ≤ 4θ(2-θ)/(1 - 2θ + 9θ² - 4θ³)时，遍历对偶间隙以O(1/k)速率收敛；当不等式严格成立时，原始-对偶迭代弱收敛到KKT点。特别地，将弱收敛理论扩展到先前未探索的区域0<θ≤1/2。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了Chambolle-Pock方法在更广泛参数范围内的统一收敛理论，为算法在0<θ≤1/2区域的收敛性提供了理论保证，扩展了现有收敛理论的应用范围，并展示了Lyapunov函数方法在分析一阶优化算法中的有效性。

Abstract: The Chambolle-Pock method, also known as the primal-dual hybrid gradient method, is a standard first-order algorithm for convex-concave saddle-point problems and composite convex optimization involving two proper, lower semicontinuous, convex functions and a bounded linear operator $L$. We study its convergence in real Hilbert spaces for step sizes $τ,σ>0$ and relaxation parameter $0<θ\le 1$. We prove that, if $τσ|L|^{2} \leq 4θ(2-θ)/(1 - 2θ+ 9θ^{2} - 4θ^{3})$, then the ergodic duality gap converges at rate $O(1/k)$, and that, when the inequality is strict, the primal-dual iterates converge weakly to a KKT point. In particular, this extends the weak-convergence theory to the previously unexplored regime $0<θ\le 1/2$. The proof is based on a Lyapunov function that remains uniformly valid over the entire interval $0<θ\le 1$.

Abstract: This paper studies probability density evolution for stochastic hybrid systems with reset maps that change the dimension of the continuous state across modes. Existing Frobenius--Perron formulations typically represent reset-induced probability transfer through boundary conditions, which is insufficient when resets map guard sets into the interior or onto lower-dimensional subsets of another mode. We develop a weak-form formulation in which reset-induced transfer is represented by the pushforward of probability flux across the guard, yielding a unified description for such systems. The proposed framework naturally captures both cases: when the reset decreases dimension, the transferred probability appears as an interior source density, whereas when the reset increases dimension, it generally appears as a singular source supported on a lower-dimensional subset. The approach is illustrated using a stochastic hybrid model in which two particles merge into one and later split back into two, demonstrating how dimension-changing resets lead to source terms beyond classical boundary-condition-based formulations.

Motivation: 研究DC算法的连续时间结构，通过将经典DCA解释为非线性自治系统的显式欧拉离散化，为理解DCA的收敛行为提供新的视角，并基于此设计改进的算法变体。

Method: 1. 在双坐标下将经典DCA解释为非线性自治系统的全步长显式欧拉离散化；2. 提出阻尼DCA方案（也是Bregman正则化DCA变体）；3. 分析其消失步长极限产生的Hessian-Riemannian梯度流；4. 建立收敛性理论框架，包括单调下降、渐近临界性、Kurdyka-Lojasiewicz收敛等。

Result: 1. 证明了阻尼DCA的单调下降、渐近临界性、有界性下的Kurdyka-Lojasiewicz收敛，以及在度量DC-PL不等式下的全局线性收敛率；2. 对极限流建立了精确能量恒等式、有界轨迹的渐近临界性、度量相对误差界下的显式全局速率、Kurdyka-Lojasiewicz假设下的有限长度和单点收敛，以及非退化局部极小值附近的局部指数收敛；3. 揭示了全局-局部权衡：半松弛方案在框架内提供最佳可证明全局保证，而全步长方案在非退化极小值附近局部最快；4. 表明不同DC分解通过凸分量生成的度量诱导不同的连续动力学，为分解质量提供几何准则。

Conclusion: 该研究通过连续时间视角为DC算法提供了新的理论框架，揭示了DCA的收敛行为与底层几何结构之间的联系，为算法设计和分解选择提供了理论指导，并将DCA与Bregman几何联系起来。

Abstract: We study the continuous-time structure of the difference-of-convex algorithm (DCA) for smooth DC decompositions with a strongly convex component. In dual coordinates, classical DCA is exactly the full-step explicit Euler discretization of a nonlinear autonomous system. This viewpoint motivates a damped DCA scheme, which is also a Bregman-regularized DCA variant, and whose vanishing-step limit yields a Hessian-Riemannian gradient flow generated by the convex part of the decomposition. For the damped scheme we prove monotone descent, asymptotic criticality, Kurdyka-Lojasiewicz convergence under boundedness, and a global linear rate under a metric DC-PL inequality. For the limiting flow we establish an exact energy identity, asymptotic criticality of bounded trajectories, explicit global rates under metric relative error bounds, finite-length and single-point convergence under a Kurdyka-Lojasiewicz hypothesis, and local exponential convergence near nondegenerate local minima. The analysis also reveals a global-local tradeoff: the half-relaxed scheme gives the best provable global guarantee in our framework, while the full-step scheme is locally fastest near a nondegenerate minimum. Finally, we show that different DC decompositions of the same objective induce different continuous dynamics through the metric generated by the convex component, providing a geometric criterion for decomposition quality and linking DCA with Bregman geometry.

</details>


### [142] [Adaptive Distributionally Robust Optimal Control with Bayesian Ambiguity Sets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06936)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有分布鲁棒最优控制模型多为离线方法，在数据稀缺时过于保守，且无法处理周期性采样场景。为克服这些限制，受Shapiro等人贝叶斯SOC框架启发，提出自适应DROC模型。

Method: 提出基于贝叶斯学习的自适应DROC模型，模糊集随新数据更新。推导易处理的风险规避重构，建立无限时域SOC的最优值函数和策略一致性，提供策略值的有限样本后验可信度保证。研究模型对样本扰动的稳定性和统计鲁棒性。开发Bellman算子割平面算法求解。

Result: 建立了理论保证：最优值函数和策略的一致性、策略值的有限样本后验可信度保证、模型对样本扰动的稳定性和统计鲁棒性。算法计算高效且收敛性可证明。库存控制问题的数值结果验证了模型和算法的有效性、自适应性和鲁棒性能。

Abstract: In stochastic optimal control (SOC), uncertainty may arise from incomplete knowledge of the true probability distribution of the underlying environment, which is known as Knightian or epistemic uncertainty. Distributionally robust optimal control (DROC) models are subsequently proposed to tackle this source of uncertainty. While such models are effective in some practical applications, most existing DROC models are offline and can be overly conservative when data are scarce. Moreover, they cannot be applied to the case when samples are generated episodically. Motivated by the Bayesian SOC framework recently proposed by Shapiro et al.~\cite{shapiro2025episodic}, we propose an adaptive DROC model in which the ambiguity set is updated via Bayesian learning from new data. Under some moderate conditions, we derive a tractable risk-averse reformulation, establish consistency of the optimal value function and optimal policy for an infinite-horizon SOC and establish a finite-sample posterior credibility guarantee for the policy value induced by the proposed episodic Bayesian DROC model. We also study the stability and statistical robustness of the proposed model with respect to sample perturbations that often arise in data-driven environments. To solve the episodic Bayesian DROC model, we propose a Bellman-operator cutting-plane (BOCP) algorithm that is computationally efficient and provably convergent. Numerical results on an inventory control problem demonstrate the effectiveness, adaptivity, and robust performance of the proposed model and algorithm.

### [143] [Model-Free Aggregative Cooperative Optimization via Randomized Gradient-Free Minimization and Exploration Momentum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07164)
*Amir Mehrnoosh,Giuseppe Speciale,Riccardo Brumali,Giuseppe Notarstefano,Gianluca Bianchin*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为ARGFree的随机无梯度算法，用于解决聚合式合作优化问题，该算法结合有限差分梯度近似和跟踪变量，并进一步提出了改进版本ARGFree-EM以提升高维环境下的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 聚合式合作优化问题出现在分布式决策环境中，每个智能体的目标函数既依赖于自身决策，也依赖于反映全局系统行为的聚合变量。实际场景中梯度信息往往不可得，因此需要开发无需梯度信息的算法来解决此类问题。

Method: ARGFree算法结合有限差分梯度近似和一组跟踪变量，模拟基于梯度的方法行为。ARGFree-EM是改进版本，在探索信号中引入动量机制，平滑梯度探索信号的突然波动，从而提高底层分布式跟踪机制的准确性。

Result: 证明了ARGFree在期望意义下收敛到一个近似最优解，近似误差源于随机梯度估计器的使用。ARGFree-EM在高维设置中表现出更好的性能。

Conclusion: ARGFree方法是文献中首个能够在不依赖梯度信息的情况下解决聚合式合作优化问题的算法类别，为分布式决策场景提供了实用的无梯度解决方案。

Abstract: Aggregative cooperative optimization problems arise in distributed decision-making settings where each agent's objective depends on its own decision as well as on an aggregate variable capturing global system behavior. Motivated by practical scenarios where gradient information is unavailable, this paper introduces a randomized gradient-free algorithm, named ARGFree, for solving such problems. ARGFree combines finite-difference gradient approximations with a set of tracking variables, emulating the behavior of a gradient-based method. We prove that ARGFree converges in expectation to an approximate optimizer, with the approximation error stemming from the use of a randomized gradient estimator. To enhance performance in high-dimensional settings, we further propose an improved variant, ARGFree-EM, which incorporates momentum in the exploration signals to smooth sudden fluctuations in the gradient exploration signals and thereby improve the accuracy of the underlying distributed tracking mechanism. To the best of our knowledge, the class of ARGFree methods is the first in the literature capable of solving aggregating cooperative optimization problems without gradient information.

We demonstrate our method's efficiency on two PDE-constrained optimization examples, showing that its performance is invariant to the PDE discretization size.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统收缩型方法通常要求单值算子满足Lipschitz连续性和单调性或共强制性条件，这限制了算法的适用范围。本文旨在开发一种更通用的方法，不依赖于这些严格条件。

Result: 算法在一般条件下获得弱收敛结果，收敛速度为O(1/√k)。当集值算子具有强单调性时，可获得强收敛结果和线性收敛速度。数值实验验证了算法在信号恢复问题中的有效性。

Abstract: This study explores an inertial-based contraction-type approach for addressing monotone variational inclusion problems (in short, MVIP) within real Hilbert spaces. Most contraction-type techniques assume Lipschitz continuity and monotonicity or co-coercivity (inverse strongly monotone) of the single-valued operator. However, the key advantage of the proposed method is that it does not rely on the coercivity condition and the Lipschitz continuity for the single-valued operator. A weak convergence result has been achieved for the proposed algorithm with a convergence rate $\mathcal{O}\left(1/\sqrt{k}\right)$. In addition, the maximal and strong monotonicity of the set-valued operator is used to establish a strong convergence result with the linear convergence rate. To demonstrate the effectiveness of our proposed method, we conduct numerical experiments focused on signal recovery problems.

### [147] [Negative curvature obstructs the existence of good barriers for interior-point methods](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07319)
*Christopher Criscitiello,Harold Nieuwboer,Michael Walter*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文证明了在双曲空间等对称Hadamard流形中，自然域（如测地球和三角形）的障碍参数随直径多项式增长，这限制了内点法在解决具有指数大直径域的缩放问题（如张量缩放）时的效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 内点法在欧几里得凸优化中表现出色，最近被扩展到Hadamard流形上的测地凸优化。然而，内点法的复杂度受限于域的障碍参数。本文旨在研究在双曲空间等对称Hadamard流形中，自然域的障碍参数如何随域直径增长，以评估内点法在解决具有大直径域的缩放问题时的适用性。

Method: 本文通过理论分析证明，在双曲空间中，包括测地球和三角形在内的几种自然域的障碍参数随域直径多项式增长。这一结果通过扩展也适用于正定矩阵和其他对称Hadamard空间。研究部分受到Hamilton和Moitra关于测地凸函数条件数下界的启发。

Result: 证明了在双曲空间中，测地球和三角形等自然域的障碍参数随直径多项式增长。这意味着依赖球障碍的内点法无法高效解决域直径可能指数级增长的挑战性缩放问题，如张量缩放问题。

Conclusion: 在对称Hadamard流形中，自然域的障碍参数随直径多项式增长，这构成了内点法的一个基本限制。对于域直径可能指数级增长的缩放问题（如张量缩放），基于这些障碍的内点法无法提供高效解决方案。这些结果补充了先前关于测地凸函数条件数下界的研究。

Abstract: Interior-point methods (IPMs) are a cornerstone of Euclidean convex optimization, due to their strong theoretical guarantees and practical performance. Motivated by scaling problems, recent work by Hirai and the last two authors (FOCS'23) extended IPMs to geodesically convex optimization on Hadamard manifolds. Crucially, the complexity of IPMs (both in Euclidean and Hadamard spaces) is governed by the \emph{barrier parameter} of the domain. Here we prove that already in hyperbolic space, several natural domains -- including geodesic balls and triangles -- have a barrier parameter that grows polynomially with the domain's diameter. By extension, the same holds for the positive-definite matrices and other symmetric Hadamard spaces. This growth implies a fundamental limitation: interior-point methods relying on barriers for a ball cannot efficiently solve challenging scaling problems, such as tensor scaling, where the domain's diameter can be exponentially large in the input size. Our results are partially inspired by, and complement, lower bounds on the condition number of geodesically convex functions established by Hamilton and Moitra (NeurIPS'21).

</details>
